You can define it as:\\n     ```\\n     reward = (positive_returns.mean() - risk_free_rate) / downside_deviation - tc_penalty * turnover\\n     where:\\n     downside_deviation = std(returns[returns < 0])\\n     ```\\n   - This penalizes only negative volatility (downside risk), aligning better with reducing harmful drawdowns.\\n\\n2. **Transaction Costs Handling**:\\n   - Instead of simple turnover penalties, implement **dynamic transaction cost penalties** proportional to trade volume:\\n     ```\\n     tc_penalty = trade_volume.sum() * cost_per_trade\\n     reward -= tc_penalty\\n     ```\\n\\nThese refinements should reduce excessive trading while aligning with downside risk objectives. Tool calls:  [ChatCompletionMessageToolCall(id='call_fQhOzFFtT4TTKg5EGptqzDDH', function=Function(arguments='{"coworker_name": "Sarah", "message": "Hi Sarah! Here are suggestions for your systematic futures strategy:\\n\\n1. **Roll Yield Estimation**:\\n   - Switch to **Nelson-Siegel-Svensson (NSS)** modeling for term structures. NSS balances backwardation and curvature better than Kalman filter fits:\\n     ```python\\n     # Pseudocode:\\n     def nss_model(parameters, time_to_maturity):\\n         beta1, beta2, beta3, tau1, tau2 = parameters\\n         return beta1 + beta2 * (1 - exp(-time_to_maturity / tau1)) / (time_to_maturity / tau1) + beta3 * exp(-time_to_maturity / tau2)\\n     ````\\n\\n2. **Basis Risk**:\\n   - Optimize roll timing and adjust for liquidity windows near delivery periods.
